Respected Dean sir,

I am writing to request a holiday on the occasion of Ram Navmi for our college. As you know, Ram Navmi is one of the most important festivals celebrated in India, and it is observed with great enthusiasm and devotion by millions of people across the country.

Ram Navmi falls on 30 march, and it would be appropriate for our college to declare a holiday on this day so that students and faculty members can observe the festival with their families and friends. It will also give everyone an opportunity to participate in the various cultural and religious activities that are organized on this occasion.

I am sure that granting a holiday on Ram Navmi will be greatly appreciated by the college community, and it will also reflect the inclusive and tolerant values that our institution upholds.

Thank you for considering my request, and I look forward to hearing from you soon.

Your Sincerely student,

Each team must consist of 7 players.

What is the Cloud?
An accessible spread network of computers that contains infrastructure and software is known as the cloud. When correctly tapped into, it has huge potential and can take people and businesses to new heights.

*30 Days of Google Cloud* gives you a chance to  start a career in the cloud and get practical  experience with the Google Cloud Platform. The fact that well-known services like YouTube, Gmail, and even the Google Search Engine operate on Google Cloud is remarkable.

With the help of the teaching platform "Qwiklabs" from Google Cloud, you may grasp computing, application development, big data, and machine learning. You are able to fully understand each of these topics by going in-depth with self-paced labs.

The most important advantages of taking part in *30 Days of Google Cloud* are learning the principles of cloud computing and setting out on an adventure to understand how the cloud actually works. A thrilling incentive is also availableâ€”you may enter to win free, unique Google prizes.

void setup(void)
{
  pinMode(A, OUTPUT);
  pinMode(B, OUTPUT);
  pinMode(C, OUTPUT);
  pinMode(D, OUTPUT);
  pinMode(E, OUTPUT);
  pinMode(F, OUTPUT);
  pinMode(G, OUTPUT);
  pinMode(H, OUTPUT);
}

//My Functions

void zero(void) {
  digitalWrite(A, HIGH);
  digitalWrite(B, HIGH);
  digitalWrite(C, HIGH);
  digitalWrite(D, HIGH);
  digitalWrite(E, HIGH);
  digitalWrite(F, HIGH);
  digitalWrite(G, LOW);
  digitalWrite(H, LOW);
}

void one(void) {
  digitalWrite(A, LOW);
  digitalWrite(B, HIGH);
  digitalWrite(C, HIGH);
  digitalWrite(D, LOW);
  digitalWrite(E, LOW);
  digitalWrite(F, LOW);
  digitalWrite(G, LOW);
  digitalWrite(H, LOW);
}

16/07/24, 10:29â€¯am - Rutvik Chavda (PPSU): const int PIN_RED   = 9; // Define constant for the red LED pin (pin 9)
const int PIN_GREEN = 10; // Define constant for the green LED pin (pin 10)
const int PIN_BLUE  = 11; // Define constant for the blue LED pin (pin 11)
  
// variables to hold our color intensities
int red;   // Variable to store the red intensity value
int green; // Variable to store the green intensity value
int blue;  // Variable to store the blue intensity value
  
/* This function "setColor" will set the color of the LED
   rather than doing it over and over in the loop. */
void setColor(int R, int G, int B) {
  analogWrite(PIN_RED,   R);   // Set the PWM value of the red LED pin to R
  analogWrite(PIN_GREEN, G);   // Set the PWM value of the green LED pin to G
  analogWrite(PIN_BLUE,  B);   // Set the PWM value of the blue LED pin to B
}
  
void setup() {
  // set all three pins to output mode
  pinMode(PIN_RED,   OUTPUT);  // Configure the red LED pin as an output
  pinMode(PIN_GREEN, OUTPUT);  // Configure the green LED pin as an output
  pinMode(PIN_BLUE,  OUTPUT);  // Configure the blue LED pin as an output
}
  
void loop() {
  // set the colors of the LED
  // Loop through Red-Green-Blue and repeat
  setColor(255, 0, 0); // Set LED to Red (max intensity for red, none for green and blue)
  delay(500);          // Wait for 500 milliseconds
  setColor(0, 255, 0); // Set LED to Green (max intensity for green, none for red and blue)
  delay(500);          // Wait for 500 milliseconds
  setColor(0, 0, 255); // Set LED to Blue (max intensity for blue, none for red and green)
  delay(500); 
  analogWrite(9,255)
  analogWrite(10,255)
  analogWrite(11,255)

  // Wait for 500 milliseconds
}

18/07/24, 1:21â€¯pm - Trupesh Patoliya (PPSU): /*
 * PIR sensor tester
 */
 
int ledPin = 13;                // choose the pin for the LED
int inputPin = 2;               // choose the input pin (for PIR sensor)
int pirState = LOW;             // we start, assuming no motion detected
int val = 0;                    // variable for reading the pin status
 
void setup() {
  pinMode(ledPin, OUTPUT);      // declare LED as output
  pinMode(inputPin, INPUT);     // declare sensor as input
 
  Serial.begin(9600);
}
 
void loop(){
  val = digitalRead(inputPin);  // read input value
  if (val == HIGH) {            // check if the input is HIGH
    digitalWrite(ledPin, HIGH);  // turn LED ON
    if (pirState == LOW) {
      
      Serial.println("Motion detected!");
      
      pirState = HIGH;
    }
  } else {
    digitalWrite(ledPin, LOW); 
    if (pirState == HIGH){
      
      Serial.println("Motion ended!");
      // We only want to print on the output change, not state
      pirState = LOW;
    }
  }
}
18/07/24, 1:33â€¯pm - Harsh Dobariya (PPSU): // Interfacing Arduino uno with LDR sensor

const int ledPin = 5; // digital pin 5 
const int ldrPin = A0; // analog pin 0

void setup() { //  Void setup function will only run once, after each powerup or reset of the Arduino board.

Serial.begin(9600);

pinMode(ledPin, OUTPUT); // Here LED is determined as an ouput or an indicator.

pinMode(ldrPin, INPUT); // Here LDR sensor is determined as input.

}

void loop() { // Void loop is ran again and again and contains main code.

int ldrStatus = analogRead(ldrPin);

if (ldrStatus <= 200) {

digitalWrite(ledPin, HIGH); // If LDR senses darkness led pin high that means led will glow.

Serial.print("Darkness over here,turn on the LED : ");

Serial.println(ldrStatus);

} else {

digitalWrite(ledPin, LOW); // If LDR senses light led pin low that means led will stop glowing.

Serial.print("There is sufficeint light , turn off the LED : ");

Serial.println(ldrStatus);

}

}

Falun Dafa, an ancient spiritual practice, rooted in the principles of Truthfulness, Compassion, and Forbearance, combines gentle exercises and meditation to improve physical and mental well-being.

This symposium aims to raise awareness about these human rights abuses and also to showcase the profound beauty and benefits of Falun Dafa.

#include <stdio.h>
//define on/off logic symbols with name ON and OFF
#define ON HIGH
#define OFF LOW
#define Sensor_Out_Pin A5
#define LED_Pin   13
 
int present_condition = 0;
int previous_condition = 0;
void setup() {
pinMode(Sensor_Out_Pin, INPUT);
pinMode(LED_Pin, OUTPUT);
}
 
void LED_Pin_blink(void);
 
void loop() {
previous_condition = present_condition;
present_condition = digitalRead(Sensor_Out_Pin); // Reading digital data from the A5 Pin of the Arduino.
 
if (previous_condition != present_condition) {
LED_Pin_blink();
 
} else {
digitalWrite(LED_Pin, OFF);
}
}
 
void LED_Pin_blink(void) {
digitalWrite(LED_Pin, ON);
delay(250);
digitalWrite(LED_Pin, OFF);
delay(250);
digitalWrite(LED_Pin, ON);
delay(250);
digitalWrite(LED_Pin, OFF);
delay(250);
}

#define DHTTYPE DHT22   // DHT 22  (AM2302)

03/09/24, 9:59â€¯am - Vatsal Savaliya: int pirPin = 10;    // PIR sensor output pin
int speakerPin = 12; // Piezo speaker pin

void setup() {
  pinMode(pirPin, INPUT);
  pinMode(speakerPin, OUTPUT);
  Serial.begin(9600);
}

void loop() {
  if (digitalRead(pirPin) == HIGH) { // If motion is detected
    digitalWrite(speakerPin, HIGH);  // Turn on the speaker
    Serial.println("Motion Detected");
    delay(1000);  // Keep the speaker on for 1 second
    digitalWrite(speakerPin, LOW);   // Turn off the speaker
  }
  else {
    digitalWrite(speakerPin, LOW);   // Ensure the speaker is off
  	Serial.println("Motion Ended");
    delay(1000);
  }
  delay(100);  // Small delay to debounce the PIR sensor
}

10/09/24, 10:22â€¯am - Nency Dhameliya: // #include <DHT22.h>

// #include "dht.h"
#include <DHT.h>

// Define the pin where the DHT sensor is connected
#define DHTPIN 2     // Digital pin 2

// Uncomment the type of sensor you're using
// #define DHTTYPE DHT11   // DHT 11
#define DHTTYPE DHT22   // DHT 22, uncomment this if using DHT22

// Initialize DHT sensor
DHT dht(DHTPIN, DHTTYPE);

void setup() {
  Serial.begin(9600);
  delay(500);  // Delay to let system boot
  Serial.println("DHT11 Humidity & Temperature Sensor\n\n");
  
  dht.begin();  // Initialize the sensor
}

void loop() {
  // Read the humidity and temperature values
  float humidity = dht.readHumidity();
  float temperature = dht.readTemperature();
  
  // Check if the readings failed
  if (isnan(humidity) || isnan(temperature)) {
    Serial.println("Failed to read from DHT sensor!");
    return;
  }

  // Print the humidity and temperature
  Serial.print("Current humidity = ");
  Serial.print(humidity);
  Serial.print("%  ");
  Serial.print("Temperature = ");
  Serial.print(temperature); 
  Serial.println("Â°C");

  delay(5000);  // Wait 5 seconds before reading again
}

    <script>
        function validateForm() {
            const name = document.getElementById("name").value;
            const addr = document.getElementById("address").value;
            const email = document.getElementById("email").value;
            const pass = document.getElementById("password").value;
            const sub = document.getElementById("subject").value;
            const agree = document.getElementById("agree").checked;

            const nameErr = document.getElementById("name-error");
            const addrErr = document.getElementById("address-error");
            const emailErr = document.getElementById("email-error");
            const passErr = document.getElementById("password-error");
            const subErr = document.getElementById("subject-error");
            const agreeErr = document.getElementById("agree-error");

            nameErr.textContent = "";
            addrErr.textContent = "";
            emailErr.textContent = "";
            passErr.textContent = "";
            subErr.textContent = "";
            agreeErr.textContent = "";

            let isValid = true;
            if (name === "" || /\d/.test(name)) {
                nameErr.textContent = "Please enter your name properly.";
                isValid = false;
            }
            if (addr === "") {
                addrErr.textContent = "Please enter your address.";
                isValid = false;
            }
            if (email === "" || !email.includes("@") || !email.includes(".")) {
                emailErr.textContent = "Please enter a valid email address.";
                isValid = false;
            }
            if (pass === "" || pass.length < 6) {
                passErr.textContent = "Please enter a password with at least 6 characters.";
                isValid = false;
            }
            if (sub === "") {
                subErr.textContent = "Please select your course.";
                isValid = false;
            }
            if (!agree) {
                agreeErr.textContent = "Please agree to the above information.";
                isValid = false;
            }
            if (isValid) {
                alert("Form submitted successfully!");
                return true;
            } else {
                return false; 
            }
        }

        function resetErrors() {
            document.getElementById("name-error").textContent = "";
            document.getElementById("address-error").textContent = "";
            document.getElementById("email-error").textContent = "";
            document.getElementById("password-error").textContent = "";
            document.getElementById("subject-error").textContent = "";
            document.getElementById("agree-error").textContent = "";
        }
    </script>
